55#ifndef HEADER_SAFESTACK_H
56# define HEADER_SAFESTACK_H
57
58# include <openssl/stack.h>
59
60#ifdef __cplusplus
61extern "C" {
62#endif
63
64# ifndef CHECKED_PTR_OF
65# define CHECKED_PTR_OF(type, p) \
66 ((void*) (1 ? p : (type*)0))
67# endif
68
69/*
70 * In C++ we get problems because an explicit cast is needed from (void *) we
71 * use CHECKED_STACK_OF to ensure the correct type is passed in the macros
72 * below.
73 */
74
75# define CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, p) \
76 ((_STACK*) (1 ? p : (STACK_OF(type)*)0))
77
78# define CHECKED_SK_COPY_FUNC(type, p) \
79 ((void *(*)(void *)) ((1 ? p : (type *(*)(const type *))0)))
80
81# define CHECKED_SK_FREE_FUNC(type, p) \
82 ((void (*)(void *)) ((1 ? p : (void (*)(type *))0)))
83
84# define CHECKED_SK_CMP_FUNC(type, p) \
85 ((int (*)(const void *, const void *)) \
86 ((1 ? p : (int (*)(const type * const *, const type * const *))0)))
87
88# define STACK_OF(type) struct stack_st_##type
89# define PREDECLARE_STACK_OF(type) STACK_OF(type);
90
91# define DECLARE_STACK_OF(type) \
92STACK_OF(type) \
93 { \
94 _STACK stack; \
95 };
96# define DECLARE_SPECIAL_STACK_OF(type, type2) \
97STACK_OF(type) \
98 { \
99 _STACK stack; \
100 };
101
102/* nada (obsolete in new safestack approach)*/
103# define IMPLEMENT_STACK_OF(type)
104
105/*-
106 * Strings are special: normally an lhash entry will point to a single
107 * (somewhat) mutable object. In the case of strings:
108 *
109 * a) Instead of a single char, there is an array of chars, NUL-terminated.
110 * b) The string may have be immutable.
111 *
112 * So, they need their own declarations. Especially important for
113 * type-checking tools, such as Deputy.
114 *
115 * In practice, however, it appears to be hard to have a const
116 * string. For now, I'm settling for dealing with the fact it is a
117 * string at all.
118 */
119typedef char *OPENSSL_STRING;
120
121typedef const char *OPENSSL_CSTRING;
122
123/*
124 * Confusingly, LHASH_OF(STRING) deals with char ** throughout, but
125 * STACK_OF(STRING) is really more like STACK_OF(char), only, as mentioned
126 * above, instead of a single char each entry is a NUL-terminated array of
127 * chars. So, we have to implement STRING specially for STACK_OF. This is
128 * dealt with in the autogenerated macros below.
129 */
130
131DECLARE_SPECIAL_STACK_OF(OPENSSL_STRING, char)
132
133/*
134 * Similarly, we sometimes use a block of characters, NOT nul-terminated.
135 * These should also be distinguished from "normal" stacks.
136 */
137typedef void *OPENSSL_BLOCK;
138DECLARE_SPECIAL_STACK_OF(OPENSSL_BLOCK, void)
139
140/*
141 * SKM_sk_... stack macros are internal to safestack.h: never use them
142 * directly, use sk_<type>_... instead
143 */
144# define SKM_sk_new(type, cmp) \
145 ((STACK_OF(type) *)sk_new(CHECKED_SK_CMP_FUNC(type, cmp)))
146# define SKM_sk_new_null(type) \
147 ((STACK_OF(type) *)sk_new_null())
148# define SKM_sk_free(type, st) \
149 sk_free(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st))
150# define SKM_sk_num(type, st) \
151 sk_num(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st))
152# define SKM_sk_value(type, st,i) \
153 ((type *)sk_value(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), i))
154# define SKM_sk_set(type, st,i,val) \
155 sk_set(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), i, CHECKED_PTR_OF(type, val))
156# define SKM_sk_zero(type, st) \
157 sk_zero(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st))
158# define SKM_sk_push(type, st, val) \
159 sk_push(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), CHECKED_PTR_OF(type, val))
160# define SKM_sk_unshift(type, st, val) \
161 sk_unshift(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), CHECKED_PTR_OF(type, val))
162# define SKM_sk_find(type, st, val) \
163 sk_find(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), CHECKED_PTR_OF(type, val))
164# define SKM_sk_find_ex(type, st, val) \
165 sk_find_ex(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), \
166 CHECKED_PTR_OF(type, val))
167# define SKM_sk_delete(type, st, i) \
168 (type *)sk_delete(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), i)
169# define SKM_sk_delete_ptr(type, st, ptr) \
170 (type *)sk_delete_ptr(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), CHECKED_PTR_OF(type, ptr))
171# define SKM_sk_insert(type, st,val, i) \
172 sk_insert(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), CHECKED_PTR_OF(type, val), i)
173# define SKM_sk_set_cmp_func(type, st, cmp) \
174 ((int (*)(const type * const *,const type * const *)) \
175 sk_set_cmp_func(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), CHECKED_SK_CMP_FUNC(type, cmp)))
176# define SKM_sk_dup(type, st) \
177 (STACK_OF(type) *)sk_dup(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st))
178# define SKM_sk_pop_free(type, st, free_func) \
179 sk_pop_free(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), CHECKED_SK_FREE_FUNC(type, free_func))
180# define SKM_sk_deep_copy(type, st, copy_func, free_func) \
181 (STACK_OF(type) *)sk_deep_copy(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), CHECKED_SK_COPY_FUNC(type, copy_func), CHECKED_SK_FREE_FUNC(type, free_func))
182# define SKM_sk_shift(type, st) \
183 (type *)sk_shift(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st))
184# define SKM_sk_pop(type, st) \
185 (type *)sk_pop(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st))
186# define SKM_sk_sort(type, st) \
187 sk_sort(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st))
188# define SKM_sk_is_sorted(type, st) \
189 sk_is_sorted(CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st))
190# define SKM_ASN1_SET_OF_d2i(type, st, pp, length, d2i_func, free_func, ex_tag, ex_class) \
191 (STACK_OF(type) *)d2i_ASN1_SET( \
192 (STACK_OF(OPENSSL_BLOCK) **)CHECKED_PTR_OF(STACK_OF(type)*, st), \
193 pp, length, \
194 CHECKED_D2I_OF(type, d2i_func), \
195 CHECKED_SK_FREE_FUNC(type, free_func), \
196 ex_tag, ex_class)
197# define SKM_ASN1_SET_OF_i2d(type, st, pp, i2d_func, ex_tag, ex_class, is_set) \
198 i2d_ASN1_SET((STACK_OF(OPENSSL_BLOCK) *)CHECKED_STACK_OF(type, st), pp, \
199 CHECKED_I2D_OF(type, i2d_func), \
200 ex_tag, ex_class, is_set)
201# define SKM_ASN1_seq_pack(type, st, i2d_func, buf, len) \
202 ASN1_seq_pack(CHECKED_PTR_OF(STACK_OF(type), st), \
203 CHECKED_I2D_OF(type, i2d_func), buf, len)
204# define SKM_ASN1_seq_unpack(type, buf, len, d2i_func, free_func) \
205 (STACK_OF(type) *)ASN1_seq_unpack(buf, len, CHECKED_D2I_OF(type, d2i_func), CHECKED_SK_FREE_FUNC(type, free_func))
206# define SKM_PKCS12_decrypt_d2i(type, algor, d2i_func, free_func, pass, passlen, oct, seq) \
207 (STACK_OF(type) *)PKCS12_decrypt_d2i(algor, \
208 CHECKED_D2I_OF(type, d2i_func), \
209 CHECKED_SK_FREE_FUNC(type, free_func), \
210 pass, passlen, oct, seq)

212 * This block of defines is updated by util/mkstack.pl, please do not touch!
213 */
